				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Magnificat in D major, BWV 243 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>12 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1732/1735

<td>12 movements:
<ol><li> Chorus: Magnificat anima mea
</li><li> Aria: Et Exultavit
</li><li> Aria: Quia respexit
</li><li> Chorus: Omnes generationes
</li><li> Aria: Quia fecit mihi magna
</li><li> Duetto: Et Misericordia
</li><li> Chorus: Fecit potentiam
</li><li> Aria: Deposuit
</li><li> Aria: Esurientes
</li><li> Terzetto: Suscepit Israel
</li><li> Chorus: Sicut locutus est
</li><li> Chorus: Gloria Patri
</li></ol>
</td></tr>

<td>1732/1735
</td></tr>

<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1733-07-02 in Leipzig, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/St._Thomas_Church,_Leipzig" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:St. Thomas Church, Leipzig">Thomaskirche</a>
<dl><dd>Soli, chorus and orchestra, J.S. Bach (conductor)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Voices:</i> 2 sopranos, alto, tenor, bass; mixed chorus (SATB)<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 oboes d’amore, (bassoon), 3 trumpets, timpani, strings, continuo
</td></tr>

</th>

<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Magnificat_(Bach)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Magnificat (Bach)">Wikipedia article</a><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jsbach.org/bwv243.html">J.S. Bach.org</a></span><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.bach.de/werk/bwv/243.htm">Bach.de (German)</a></span><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.sheetmusicplus.com/composers/johann-sebastian-bach-sheet-music/1800148?Ntt=Magnificat&amp;narrow_by=Magnificat&amp;Ns=default&amp;recsPerPage=50&amp;id=298930"><i>Magnificat</i> - scores at Sheet Music Plus</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>The original version—<i><a href="/wiki/Magnificat_in_E-flat_major,_BWV_243a_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Magnificat in E-flat major, BWV 243a (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Magnificat in E-flat major</a></i>—was first performed on Christmas Day, 1723 at the Thomaskirche in Leipzig under the composer's direction. The work was subsequently revised (1728–31) and performed in its present version in 1733.
</td></tr></table>
